< review>
I was born in Point Pleasant and have been to the original and I've been to a few other Jersey Mikes in California since they have opened some stores out here and this store is one of the worst. It is a glorified Subway, cheap on everything. You see those pictures, well their subs look nothing like those pictures. I've been to this location twice and both times the subs were not very good. The first time the bread was not fresh and was kind of hard. The sub I got from both visits barely had any toppings, maybe there were a few pieces of onions on it. I had to search for them because you could not tell. There was hardly any lettuce on it, a typical Jersey mikes sub does not skimp on these topping and if anything you have to ask for them to go light, well this location, you would swear there was a huge shortage on lettuce and onions, I guess at least they still covered it length wise with tomatoes. Overall, I was really disappointed in the quality of the sub at this location. Other locations are better than this one. One in Mountain View was probably the best and closest to the original I have been to out here.<//review>

I only recently started eating at Jersey Mike's, before this location opened. I'd go to the one in Rocklin, but we were treated poorly by the staff, as if we were bothering them by coming in for a sandwich. Once this location opened I have only been treated with the best customer service. The owner is often there and makes sure to greet everyone and learn their orders if they come often enough. <text>My husband and I have been going to this Tiffany's store for a few years now, to get charms for my bracelet on special occasions, which was also purchased here. We have spent hundreds and hundreds of dollars there, over that period of time. On November 5th, we made a trip there for my birthday, and when we walked up to the door, the door attendant was extremely rude, and it took us both aback, to the point that I was speechless for a moment. The first words out of his mouth weren't a greeting, like you would expect from an upscale store like this, he actually said, very loudly, without a bit of couth, "what are you here for?" And then when I couldn't find an answer because I was stunned, he got agitated, and said in a very condescending tone, "to shop or what??" I was floored! I did not get his name, but he was African- American. We drove close to two hours to go to this location for my birthday, when we could have gone to a store in Sacramento that's only an hour away, because we like this store, but he dampened our mood for sure. I gave the two stars for the salesman that helped us once we were actually in the store because he was very friendly and helpful. To sum this up, the door attendant needs a brush up on courtesy and professionalism when dealing with customers, because his behavior was unacceptable.<//text>< user>

I have been shopping at Tiffany since 2009 and after moving to the Bay Area I have visited this located many times to make purchases and to get my wife's items checked. I worked with a great consultant via email to help find the right ring, and after many email exchanges, I went in and got the ring picked, ordered, and it came in perfect. < review>
Sonic is always a good late night stop. If you have time and don't need to be anywhere soon, pull into the parking spot and order/eat in the car. If you're on the move and can deal with a 5 minute wait then go for the drive thru. Be aware, on busy nights when the staff coverage isn't the best the wait can be exceedingly long, but this has only happened once for me. Great place, great food, fun to partake in. Bring skates back!< /review>
